CREATE TABLE wms_addressee_code
(
  id bigint NOT NULL,
  discriminator character varying(255) NOT NULL,
  plant_id bigint,
  code character varying(50) NOT NULL,
  pro_code character varying(255),
  city_code character varying(255),
  pro_name character varying(255),
  city_name character varying(255),
  create_operator_id bigint,
  create_operator_name character varying(50),
  create_time timestamp without time zone,
  update_operator_id bigint,
  update_operator_name character varying(50),
  update_time timestamp without time zone,
  CONSTRAINT wms_addressee_code_pkey PRIMARY KEY (id),
  CONSTRAINT fk5115d81a8eeaec98 FOREIGN KEY (plant_id)
      REFERENCES wms_plant (id) MATCH SIMPLE
      ON UPDATE NO ACTION ON DELETE NO ACTION
)
WITH (
  OIDS=FALSE
);
